                <h1 class="headline ">
                 <a class="js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=a_top_hero&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/story/2018/07/27/federal-housing-chief-sexual-harassment-investigation-714779" target="_top">

                 </a>

             <h1 class="headline ">

               ‘We are fighting for information about war’: Pentagon curbs media access
              </a>
             </h1>
             <div class="tease">
